SUBJECT:         MABEL / October Fun

Hi Lori -<p>Mabel - the little star - is all set for October.  More fun awaits.<p>Mabel is doing really well - she's loves her friends and although little - she is showing that she is quite mighty with the bigger dogs!<p>Not a huge deal, though - Ashley bumped into your neighbor the other day and she said that she walks Mabel from time to time and walks her on the right.  Dogs are traditionally taught to walk on the left (a history lesson - dogs were taught to walk on the left/heel so that - in Victorian times - the dog would be walking in the street and thus could poop in the street rather than the sidewalk or a garden).  Also, to manage the group - if they're all walking on the left, the unruly mob is more manageable.  If it's a problem, no need to mention - AT ALL (I know how neighbors can be :)  to your neighbor.  In Ashleys retelling of the meeting with the neighbor, it seemed like

Unfortunately, we can not be responsible.  It took TWO pet sitters and almost an hour to get it inside because it was oversized.  We will not be able to do this in the future.  <p>We have also had packages delivered that needed to be placed in a refrigerator or freezer right away.  We are very happy to do this if the ENTIRE box will fit in the refrigerator or freezer.  We can not rearrange your refrigerator or freezer for the box to fit.  We can NOT open any packages to make items fit.   We will not be responsible for any items that 
need to be refrigerated or frozen.  <p>It will be your responsibility to arrange for these packages to be delivered after you arrive home or have a friend, neighbor or relative stop by to take care of it.   <p>If we must contact you via email or phone, and it is OUTSIDE of our call back times, there will be an extra charge for the office to to do this.<p>Remember, our service is not package or mail delivery. function firstAppointmentCheck() {
  if(document.itinerary != undefined) 
  	document.itinerary.startingaddress.disabled = document.itinerary.firstappointmentstart.checked;
}
function move(change, index) {
	document.itinerary.change.value = change;
	document.itinerary.index.value = index;
	document.itinerary.submit();
}

function highlightRow(row,onOff) {
	color = onOff ? 'lightgreen' : 'white';
	key = row.id.split('_');
	key = key[0];
	//alert(key);
	document.getElementById(key+'_top').style.background = color;
	for(var i=0; document.getElementById(key+'_'+i); i++)
	  document.getElementById(key+'_'+i).style.background = color;
}

function generateDirections() {
	
	//alert("Temporarily unavailable.");
	//return;
	
	document.itinerary.generate.value = 1;
	document.itinerary.submit();
}

function sendToProvider() {
	document.itinerary.generate.value = 0;
	document.itinerary.emailprovider.value = 1;
	document.itinerary.submit();
}

firstAppointmentCheck();
</script>
